$CATEGORY: $course$ / Examples / Arrays1

::Arrays Level 1 #000::
What are the contents of the array after the following statements?
<pre>int list[6] = \{8, 0, 6, 5, 7, 3\};
int temp;
temp = list[3];
list[3] = list[2];
list[2] = temp;</pre>
	{
	=\{8, 0, 5, 6, 7, 3\}
	~\{8, 0, 6, 5, 7, 3\}
	~\{8, 6, 6, 5, 5, 3\}
	~\{8, 6, 0, 5, 7, 3\}
	~\{8, 0, 6, 7, 5, 3\}
	}

::Arrays Level 1 #001::
What are the contents of the array after the following statements?
<pre>int dogs[5] = \{8, 5, 4, 7, 3\};
int temp;
temp = dogs[1];
dogs[1] = dogs[3];
dogs[3] = temp;</pre>
	{
	=\{8, 7, 4, 5, 3\}
	~\{8, 5, 4, 7, 3\}
	~\{8, 5, 3, 7, 3\}
	~\{4, 5, 8, 7, 3\}
	~\{8, 5, 3, 7, 4\}
	}
